File: SMESQUAD.HIS     Last update: 3/13/2012 John P. Anderson

HISTORY LOG

Data set: SMES Vegetation Quadrat Data
Project:  Small Mammal Exclosure Study
Responsible investigator: David Lightfoot

NOTE: Sorted by: year, season, site, block, plot, quad, species,
      then line number.

NOTE:
8/23/2000 John Anderson
SMAMEX S99 data: Grassland site, Block 3, Plot 1 is missing from the entered
data set.  It is also missing from the tape label information recorded by the
readers in the field.  All other data was accounted for using the tape label
information.


Variable description:
   DATE    - Date data was collected
   S       - Site location code [C=Creosotebush, G=Grassland]
   B       - Block Number [1-4]
   P       - Plot number [1-4]
   T       - Treatment type [C=Control, R=Rodent Exclosuer, L=Laghmorph
             Exclosure, B=Bovine Exclosure
   QD      - Quad number [1-36]
   SPP     - Species Code, see SMESSPP.LST for complete species code
            listing.
   ID#     - Book -or- Tape Number
   COMMENTS
   L       - Line number for individual comment
